scribe::headers.introduction

scribe::base_url: http://127.0.0.1:8000

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

scribe::headers.auth

scribe::auth.instruction.bearer

scribe::auth.details

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Endpoints

POST api/v1/me/upload

requires authentication

scribe::example_request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/me/upload" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"file\": \"jrezqwkhmanfoqcxzjjwdtb\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/me/upload"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "file": "jrezqwkhmanfoqcxzjjwdtb"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
scribe::try_it_out.received_response:
scribe::try_it_out.request_failed:


scribe::try_it_out.error_help

scribe::endpoint.request      

POST api/v1/me/upload

scribe::endpoint.headers

Authorization      

Example: Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

scribe::endpoint.body_parameters

uuid   string  optional  
name   string  optional  
custom_properties   string  optional  
file   string   

گزینه value نباید بزرگتر از 102400 کاراکتر باشد. Example: jrezqwkhmanfoqcxzjjwdtb

GET api/v1/me

requires authentication

scribe::example_request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/me" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/me"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

POST api/v1/me

requires authentication

scribe::example_request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/me" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"zachary.cassin@example.net\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/me"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "zachary.cassin@example.net"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

scribe::endpoint.headers

Authorization      

Example: Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

scribe::endpoint.body_parameters

first_name   string  optional  
last_name   string  optional  
national_number   string  optional  
state_id   string  optional  
city_id   string  optional  
email   string  optional  

گزینه value باید یک آدرس ایمیل صحیح باشد. Example: zachary.cassin@example.net

mobile   string  optional  
password   string  optional  
confirm   string  optional  

This field is required when password is present. The value and password must match.

gender   string  optional  
avatar   string  optional

POST api/v1/cart/address

requires authentication

scribe::example_request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/cart/address" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"address_id\": \"officia\",
    \"type\": \"alias\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/cart/address"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "address_id": "officia",
    "type": "alias"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

);

}).then(response => response.json());

GET api/v1/search

requires authentication

scribe::example_request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/search" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"q\": \"assumenda\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/search"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer 504|enI0PVD9wikSHlb68wp3URvWRAbxkQ2GB9nExV3Q",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "q": "assumenda"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
